   1              	﻿;/*"++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++"
   0              	
   0              	
   2              	;@"																			"			
   3              	;@"      Filename: smartstart64.s											"
   4              	;@"      Copyright(c): Leon de Boer(LdB) 2017								"
   5              	;@"      Version: 2.03														"
   6              	;@"																			"		
   7              	;@"***************[ THIS CODE IS FREEWARE UNDER CC Attribution]*************"
   8              	;@"																            "
   9              	;@"     This sourcecode is released for the purpose to promote programming  "
  10              	;@"  on the Raspberry Pi. You may redistribute it and/or modify with the    "
  11              	;@"  following disclaimer and condition.                                    "
  12              	;@"																            "
  13              	;@"      The SOURCE CODE is distributed "AS IS" WITHOUT WARRANTIES AS TO    "
  14              	;@"   PERFORMANCE OF MERCHANTABILITY WHETHER EXPRESSED OR IMPLIED.          "
  15              	;@"   Redistributions of source code must retain the copyright notices to   "
  16              	;@"   maintain the author credit (attribution) .							"
  17              	;@"																			"
  18              	;@"*************************************************************************"
  19              	;@"                                                                         "
  20              	;@"       This code expands on my earlier SmartStart bootstub assembler for "
  21              	;@" the Pi3. It directly supports multicore operation in C/C++. To do that  "
  22              	;@" it provides stack space to each core and provides a modified bootloader " 
  23              	;@" spinlock that protects against registers X0-X7 trashed. As any C/C++    "
  24              	;@" 64 bit compiler will trash those registers, to use C/C++ in multicore   "
  25              	;@" programming this protection must be done.								"
  26              	;@"       This is a matching paired AARCH64 stub for the 64bit linker file  "
  27              	;@" and carries the samme arrangement as AARCH32 to ease porting.		    "
  28              	;@"																            "
  29              	;@"+++++++++++++++++++++++[ REVISIONS ]+++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++"
  30              	;@"  1.01 Initial release .. Pi autodetection main aim                      "
  31              	;@"  1.02 Many functions moved out C to aide 32/64 bit compatability        "
  32              	;@"  2.01 Futher reductions to bare minmum assembeler code                  "
  33              	;@"  2.02 Multicore functionality added                                     "
  34              	;@"  2.03 Timer Irq support added  											"
  35              	;@"+++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++"*/
  36              	
  37              	.section ".text.startup", "ax", %progbits
  38              	.balign	4
  39              	.globl _start
  40              	_start:	
  41 0000 0C000010 		adr x12, _start							// Hold boot address in high register R12
  42 0004 610D0058 		ldr x1, =RPi_BootAddr					// Address of RPi_BootAddr
  43 0008 2C0000B9 		str w12, [x1]							// Store the boot address
  44              	
  45 000c 600D0058 		ldr	x0, =0x3F000000						// No need to detect address in 64bit mode it has to be 0x3F000000 on Pi3
  46 0010 810D0058 		ldr x1, =RPi_IO_Base_Addr				// Address of RPi_IO_Base_Addr
  47 0014 200000B9 		str w0, [x1]							// Store the IO base address
  48              	
  49 0018 200080D2 		mov x0, #1								// Multicore support starts as 1 core
  50 001c 610D0058 		ldr x1, =RPi_CoresReady					// Address of RPi_CoresReady
  51 0020 200000B9 		str w0, [x1]							// Store the CoresReady count as 1
  52              	
  53 0024 001380D2 		mov x0, #0x98							// Compiled for ARM8 CPU in AARCH64 and supports 4 cores
  54 0028 410D0058 		ldr x1, =RPi_CompileMode				// Address of RPi_CompileMode

  78 0058 420C0058 	    ldr x2, = __EL2_stack_core0				// Address of EL2_stack_core0 stack pointer value

  80 0060 840C0058 	    ldr x4, = __EL0_stack_core0				// Address of EL0_stack_core0 stack pointer value

  85 0074 630C0058 	    ldr x3, = __EL1_stack_core1				// Address of EL1_stack_core1 stack pointer value

  92 0090 DF0800F1 		cmp x6, #2								// Check cpu id for core 2

  95 009c A30C0058 	    ldr x3, = __EL1_stack_core3				// Address of EL1_stack_core3 stack pointer value
  96 00a0 C40C0058 	    ldr x4, = __EL0_stack_core3				// Address of EL0_stack_core3 stack pointer value

 127              	//"================================================================"
 128              	    /*  RES1 bits (29,28,23,22,20,11) to 1
 129              		 *  RES0 bits (31,30,27,21,17,13,10,6) +
 130              		 *  UCI,EE,EOE,WXN,nTWE,nTWI,UCT,DZE,I,UMA,SED,ITD,
 131              		 *  CP15BEN,SA0,SA,C,A,M to 0 */

 135 00e8 000074B2 		orr    x0, x0, #(0x1 << 12)           // The I bit on (instruction cache)
 136 00ec 001018D5 		msr	sctlr_el1, x0

 138              	//"================================================================"
 139              	//  Return to the EL1_SP1 mode from EL2 for all Cores
 140              	//"================================================================"

 193              	#define spin_cpu2 0xe8
